CREATE TABLE Roles (role_id INT PRIMARY KEY, role_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL)

CREATE TABLE UserRoles (user_id INT, role_id INT, PRIMARY KEY (user_id, role_id))</t><s>SELECT user_id, MAX(role_id) AS max_role_id FROM UserRoles GROUP BY user_id ORDER BY max_role_id DESC LIMIT 10</s>
